<Resp>None</Resp><Rate>1<//Rate>< review>
Saturday night.  Not very busy.  At least 12 empty tables.  Service was HORRENDOUS.  When you charge full fare for an 8 year old to eat, your service should be full fare also.  I can get past the fact that the server was, apparently, a trainee.  But, when 3 different people pass my table and can't see that there are 3 empty water glasses, I'm wondering what the problem is.  And when the woman, that passed my table 3 times while the glasses were empty, and only stopped to turn down the fire (which only made for longer cook times), kept glaring at us, it only served to exacerbate the situation. The only time anyone showed a real urgency in getting to our table was when my son got fed up with waiting for water and went and got 2 pitchers and brought them to the table.  Suddenly we had 3 people eager to see about us.

And so all is clear, just 1 week earlier, we went to another restaurant 35 miles away, and spent $80 for 4 people.  After a 2 hour wait Boiling Crab was stupendous.  Phenomenal service and great food.  For which we happily tipped 25%.

Bottom line... $68 for crap service and marginally decent food.  Last time I'll ever go there.
I guess that's what I get for trying to patronize businesses in my neighborhood.  Next time I'll just go to the place I like in Cerritos.  Less expensive.  Better service.  And a FAR better experience.

And I've already told at least 5 people about the crappy experience.  I will be telling more people.  And if you are Belllko, you know exactly which 3 people were at your restaurant on Saturday night, 2/21/15.  And you know why there was no tip left.  Keep your preformed notions to yourself.  YOU are the reason there was no tip.

I FORGOT TO MENTION...
The shears for cutting the meat were FILTHY!!!!!
And when I asked for another pair, from the glaring broad, she came back with another pair that was even nastier.  I guess dish water is in as short supply as drinking water.< /review>

Such authentic setting, food and service.  You feel like you've walked into a wonderfully special, intimate restaurant in Rome or Florence, with unpainted wood trim around windows and doors and warm wall decor.  All the servings are what I can only call succulent: moist, luscious, fresh.  And all of the servers and back up staff make you feel like you're the most important person in the room.  I LOVE this place...so lucky to have it here in SF.</review>

< Review>
Had 4 items, all superb.  The memories from our last trip to SF have consolidated to very few, this restaurant being one of them.  Make a reservation early and enjoy the experience of a unique, Italian American, family run, small, scratch restaurant serving properly fresh and fundamentally prepared food.  Don't let the awkward bathroom or curt staff throw you off, it is a great time.</Review>

We were visiting West Hollywood and looking for something yummy, somehow ended up here. First time here and food was fine. Service was okay but In all fairness to our waiter, the restaurant was busy. The hostess not so friendly but it was late so she could have had a long day. I had the bean and cheese chimichanga, it was okay. <Text>Good quality food, decent prices and large portions. Nothing life-changing, just the basic Mexican food you can find anywhere.

Mr. M got the Cobb Salad which was loaded with bacon and cheese. Mom did a lunch special -$5.95 for a tamale with rice and beans. It said you could choose any meat, but she was informed that only Chicken was available that day (a Friday). Hubby got the shrimp fajitas because it was Lent. He enjoyed it, but seemed particularly smitten with the warm tortilla chips and the freshness of the salsa.

I got the cheese Nachos. Just tortilla chips covered in melted cheese, not disgusting cheese sauce. It also came with guacamole. Again, nothing life changing, just exactly what I expected. But I certainly appreciated the extra thick layer of cheese on top (even if the chips on the bottom layer were left naked).

Service was very fast and friendly.< /Text><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>
